  <script>
   function showDesc(id)
{
     if (document.getElementById(id).style.display == 'none')
     {
          document.getElementById(id).style.display = 'block';
          document.getElementById('cat_short_descr').style.display = 'none';

     }
}

function hideDesc(id)
{
     if (document.getElementById(id).style.display == 'none')
     {
          document.getElementById(id).style.display = 'none';
          document.getElementById('cat_short_descr').style.display = 'block';
     }
     else
     {
          document.getElementById(id).style.display = 'none';
          document.getElementById('cat_short_descr').style.display = 'block';
     }
}
  </script>

               <!-- homepage content -->
               <div id="home_short_descr">
                Fabricville was established in 1970 when Fabricland, the largest fabric store in Canada, decided to expand to Quebec. With 23 stores throughout Quebec and Eastern Canada, Fabricville has been the number one source for fabrics and draperies for the past 45 years.
                <p>
                 <a href="javascript:showDesc('home_descr');">
                  read more
                 </a>
                </p>
               </div>
               <div id="home_descr" style="display:none;">
                <p>
                 By combining our buying power with Fabricland and buying directly from the source, we ensure that our customers get the best value for their dollar. This unique national buying power allows our fabric store to offer our consumers competitive prices at significant savings. With our long-lasting relationships with international mills, Fabricville can make the largest selection of fabric collections affordable for many customers. In addition to Fabricville’s own exclusive fabric collections, we also carry brands such as Jaclyn Smith, Waverly, Michael Miller, Henry Glass, and a variety of licensed products from Disney and Marvel.
                </p>
                <p>
                 Value is not the only factor that makes Fabricville the leader in the fabric industry. Staying current is equally as important. That is why our team of buyers travel the world in search of the latest trends to bring the most up-to date merchandise to our customers. Fabricville offers a huge selection of fabrics to fit every taste and budget. The choices are endless whether a customer is opting to make a garment, a quilt, a craft, a knitting project or their own window coverings. Fabricville offers consumers the materials and the inspiration they need to create something unique and beautiful.
                </p>
                <p>
                 Everyone knows that Fabricville is the place for all your sewing needs but in recent years our fabric stores have expanded to become a full service window-covering destination. 
        When it comes to window coverings, we offer both in-store and in-home consultation services. Our staff is very knowledgeable and can offer consumers design ideas within any set budget. If you cannot personally visit one of the many locations, Fabricville offers an interactive website that helps you select fabrics or custom blinds and visualise your window coverings from the comfort of your own home. This online custom drapery site was launched in 2010 and has successfully serviced many customers looking for custom blinds and unique custom draperies.
                </p>
                <p>
                 In 2014, Fabricville launched a completely new and redesigned e-commerce website. This came about as a response to a growing consumer need from rural areas of Quebec and Easter Canada to make Fabricville’s products available to them. With this in mind, our online fabric store was launched to service not only these customers but also customers across the country and around the world. 
        Fabricville stocks the largest inventory of fashion fabrics, fleece and flannelettes in the country, as well as an extensive selection of drapery and upholstery fabrics. The online fabric store focuses on offering customers the best selection of fabrics for fashion, home décor, crafts and quilting as well as sewing notions patterns, drapery hardware, accents and accessories. It is this vast choice combined with the value that sets Fabricville apart from the competition, servicing not only the Canadian market but also the American and European fabric enthusiasts.
        The online fabric store not only allows customers to order merchandise but also serves as a source of valuable information for fabric care, window covering tips and ‘Do it yourself’ projects.
                </p>
                <p>
                 Your positive shopping experience means everything to us and that is why we have stood by our mission statement for the last 45 years. Please let us hear about your shopping experiences by clicking
                 <a href="/en/contacts">
                  here
                 </a>
                </p>
                <p>
                 Fabricville`s Mission: We are committed to deliver exceptional customer service.
                </p>
                <a href="javascript:hideDesc('home_descr');">
                 close
                </a>
               </div>
              </div>
